<a name="networking"></a> 
### <a name="networking"></a><span data-ttu-id="63064-925">네트워킹</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-925">Networking</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="63064-926">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]에서는 HTTP 응용 프로그램의 새로운 프로그래밍 인터페이스를 제공합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-926">The [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] provides a new programming interface for HTTP applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-927">자세한 내용은 새로운 <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> 및 <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType> 네임스페이스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-927">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.Http?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Net.Http.Headers?displayProperty=nameWithType> namespaces.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="63064-928">기존의 <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> 및 관련 클래스를 사용하여 WebSocket 연결을 허용하고 이와 상호 작용하는 새로운 프로그래밍 인터페이스 지원도 포함되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-928">Support is also included for a new programming interface for accepting and interacting with a WebSocket connection by using the existing <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> and related classes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-929">자세한 내용은 새로운 <xref:System.Net.WebSockets> 네임스페이스 및 <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> 클래스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-929">For more information, see the new <xref:System.Net.WebSockets> namespace and the <xref:System.Net.HttpListener> class.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="63064-930">또한 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]에는 다음 네트워킹 개선 사항이 포함되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-930">In addition, the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] includes the following networking improvements:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-931">RFC 규격 URI 지원.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-931">RFC-compliant URI support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-932">자세한 내용은 <xref:System.Uri> 및 관련 클래스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-932">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-933">IDN(Internationalized Domain Name) 구문 분석 지원.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-933">Support for Internationalized Domain Name (IDN) parsing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-934">자세한 내용은 <xref:System.Uri> 및 관련 클래스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-934">For more information, see <xref:System.Uri> and related classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-935">EAI(Email Address Internationalization) 지원.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-935">Support for Email Address Internationalization (EAI).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-936">자세한 내용은 <xref:System.Net.Mail> 네임스페이스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-936">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Mail> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-937">IPv6 지원 개선.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-937">Improved IPv6 support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-938">자세한 내용은 <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation> 네임스페이스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-938">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.NetworkInformation> namespace.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-939">이중 모드 소켓 지원.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-939">Dual-mode socket support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-940">자세한 내용은 <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket> 및 <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener> 클래스를 참조하세요.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-940">For more information, see the <xref:System.Net.Sockets.Socket> and <xref:System.Net.Sockets.TcpListener> classes.</span></span>

<a name="client"></a> 
### <a name="windows-presentation-foundation-wpf"></a><span data-ttu-id="63064-941">WPF(Windows Presentation Foundation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-941">Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="63064-942">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]의 WPF(Windows Presentation Foundation)에서 변경되고 개선된 영역은 다음과 같습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-942">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], Windows Presentation Foundation (WPF) contains changes and improvements in the following areas:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-943">빠른 실행 도구 모음, 응용 프로그램 메뉴 및 탭을 호스팅하는 리본 사용자 인터페이스 구현에 사용할 수 있는 새로운 <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> 컨트롤</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-943">The new <xref:System.Windows.Controls.Ribbon.Ribbon> control, which enables you to implement a ribbon user interface that hosts a Quick Access Toolbar, Application Menu, and tabs.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-944">동기 및 비동기 데이터 유효성 검사를 지원하는 새로운 <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> 인터페이스</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-944">The new <xref:System.ComponentModel.INotifyDataErrorInfo> interface, which supports synchronous and asynchronous data validation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-945"><xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> 및 <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> 클래스의 새로운 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-945">New features for the <xref:System.Windows.Controls.VirtualizingPanel> and <xref:System.Windows.Threading.Dispatcher> classes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-946">그룹화된 큰 데이터 집합을 표시하고 UI가 아닌 스레드에서 컬렉션에 액세스할 때의 성능 개선</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-946">Improved performance when displaying large sets of grouped data, and by accessing collections on non-UI threads.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-947">정적 속성에 대한 데이터 바인딩, <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> 인터페이스를 구현하는 사용자 지정 형식에 대한 데이터 바인딩 및 바인딩 식에서 데이터 바인딩 정보 검색</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-947">Data binding to static properties, data binding to custom types that implement the <xref:System.Reflection.ICustomTypeProvider> interface, and retrieval of data binding information from a binding expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-948">값이 변경될 때(라이브 셰이핑) 데이터의 위치 변경</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-948">Repositioning of data as the values change (live shaping).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-949">항목 컨테이너에 대한 데이터 컨텍스트 연결을 해제할지 여부를 확인하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-949">Ability to check whether the data context for an item container is disconnected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-950">속성 변경과 데이터 소스 업데이트 간에 경과되어야 하는 시간을 설정하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-950">Ability to set the amount of time that should elapse between property changes and data source updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-951">취약한 이벤트 패턴을 구현하기 위한 지원 개선.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-951">Improved support for implementing weak event patterns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-952">또한 이벤트가 태그 확장을 수락할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-952">Also, events can now accept markup extensions.</span></span>

<a name="windows_communication_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-communication-foundation-wcf"></a><span data-ttu-id="63064-953">WCF(Windows Communication Foundation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-953">Windows Communication Foundation (WCF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="63064-954">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]에서 WCF(Windows Communication Foundation) 응용 프로그램을 더 쉽게 작성하고 유지 관리할 수 있도록 다음 기능이 추가되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-954">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], the following features have been added to make it simpler to write and maintain Windows Communication Foundation (WCF) applications:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-955">생성된 구성 파일의 단순화</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-955">Simplification of generated configuration files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-956">계약 중심 개발 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-956">Support for contract-first development.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-957">ASP.NET 호환성 모드를 더 쉽게 구성하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-957">Ability to configure ASP.NET compatibility mode more easily.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-958">기본 전송 속성 값을 변경하여 값을 설정해야 할 가능성을 줄임</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-958">Changes in default transport property values to reduce the likelihood that you will have to set them.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-959"><xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> 클래스를 업데이트하여 XML 사전 판독기에 대해 수동으로 할당량을 구성해야 할 가능성을 줄임</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-959">Updates to the <xref:System.Xml.XmlDictionaryReaderQuotas> class to reduce the likelihood that you will have to manually configure quotas for XML dictionary readers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-960">Visual Studio에서 빌드 프로세스의 일부로 WCF 구성 파일의 유효성 검사를 실시하여 응용 프로그램 실행 전에 구성 오류를 검색할 수 있도록 함</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-960">Validation of WCF configuration files by Visual Studio as part of the build process, so you can detect configuration errors before you run your application.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-961">새로운 비동기 스트리밍 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-961">New asynchronous streaming support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-962">새 HTTPS 프로토콜 매핑을 사용하면 간단하게 IIS(인터넷 정보 서비스)로 HTTPS에서 끝점을 표시할 수 있음</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-962">New HTTPS protocol mapping to make it easier to expose an endpoint over HTTPS with Internet Information Services (IIS).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-963">서비스 URL에 `?singleWSDL`을 추가하여 단일 WSDL 문서에서 메타데이터를 생성하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-963">Ability to generate metadata in a single WSDL document by appending `?singleWSDL` to the service URL.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-964">Websocket이 포트 80 및 443에서 완벽한 양방향 통신을 지원하며 성능 특성은 TCP 전송과 유사함</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-964">Websockets support to enable true bidirectional communication over ports 80 and 443 with performance characteristics similar to the TCP transport.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-965">코드에서 서비스 구성 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-965">Support for configuring services in code.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-966">XML 편집기 도구 설명</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-966">XML Editor tooltips.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-967"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> 캐싱 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-967"><xref:System.ServiceModel.ChannelFactory> caching support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-968">이진 인코더 압축 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-968">Binary encoder compression support.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-969">개발자가 "실행 후 제거" 메시징을 사용하는 서비스를 작성할 수 있는 UDP 전송 지원.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-969">Support for a UDP transport that enables developers to write services that use "fire and forget" messaging.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-970">클라이언트는 서비스에 메시지를 보내고 서비스에서 응답을 기대하지 않습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-970">A client sends a message to a service and expects no response from the service.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-971">HTTP 전송 및 전송 보안 사용 시 단일 WCF 끝점에 대한 여러 인증 모드를 지원하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-971">Ability to support multiple authentication modes on a single WCF endpoint when using the HTTP transport and transport security.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-972">IDN(Internationalized Domain Name)을 사용하는 WCF 서비스 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-972">Support for WCF services that use internationalized domain names (IDNs).</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="63064-973">자세한 내용은 [Windows Communication Foundation의 새로운 기능](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173)을 참조하십시오.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-973">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Communication Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228173).</span></span>

<a name="windows_workflow_foundation"></a> 
### <a name="windows-workflow-foundation-wf"></a><span data-ttu-id="63064-974">Windows WF(Workflow Foundation)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-974">Windows Workflow Foundation (WF)</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="63064-975">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]의 Windows WF(Workflow Foundation)에 몇 가지 새로운 기능이 추가되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-975">In the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)], several new features were added to Windows Workflow Foundation (WF), including:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-976">상태 시스템 워크플로가 .NET Framework 4.0.1([.NET Framework 4 플랫폼 업데이트 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092))의 일부로 처음 도입됨.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-976">State machine workflows, which were first introduced as part of the .NET Framework 4.0.1 ([.NET Framework 4 Platform Update 1](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkID=215092)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-977">이 업데이트에는 개발자가 상태 시스템 워크플로를 만들 수 있도록 하는 몇 가지 새로운 클래스와 활동이 포함되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-977">This update included several new classes and activities that enabled developers to create state machine workflows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-978">이러한 클래스와 활동은 다음을 포함하도록 [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)]에 대해 업데이트되었습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-978">These classes and activities were updated for the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] to include:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-979">상태에 중단점을 설정하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-979">The ability to set breakpoints on states.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-980">Workflow Designer에서 전환을 복사하여 붙여 넣는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-980">The ability to copy and paste transitions in the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-981">공유 트리거 전환 작성을 위한 디자이너 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-981">Designer support for shared trigger transition creation.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-982"><xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State> 및 <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>을 포함하는 상태 시스템 워크플로를 만들기 위한 활동</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-982">Activities for creating state machine workflows, including: <xref:System.Activities.Statements.StateMachine>, <xref:System.Activities.Statements.State>, and <xref:System.Activities.Statements.Transition>.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-983">다음과 같은 향상된 Workflow Designer 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-983">Enhanced Workflow Designer features such as the following:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-984">Visual Studio의 **빠른 찾기** 및 **파일에서 찾기** 등의 향상된 워크플로 검색 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-984">Enhanced workflow search capabilities in Visual Studio, including **Quick Find** and **Find in Files**.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-985">컨테이너 활동에 두 번째 자식 활동이 추가될 때 Sequence 활동을 자동으로 생성하고 두 활동 모두를 Sequence 활동에 포함하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-985">Ability to automatically create a Sequence activity when a second child activity is added to a container activity, and to include both activities in the Sequence activity.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-986">스크롤 막대를 사용하지 않고 워크플로의 보이는 부분을 변경할 수 있는 이동 기능 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-986">Panning support, which enables the visible portion of a workflow to be changed without using the scroll bars.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-987">트리 스타일 개요 뷰에서 워크플로의 구성 요소를 보여 주는 새로운 **문서 개요** 뷰. 이 **문서 개요** 뷰에서 구성 요소를 선택할 수 있음</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-987">A new **Document Outline** view that shows the components of a workflow in a tree-style outline view and lets you select a component in the **Document Outline** view.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-988">활동에 주석을 추가하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-988">Ability to add annotations to activities.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-989">Workflow Designer를 사용하여 활동 대리자를 정의하고 사용하는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-989">Ability to define and consume activity delegates by using the workflow designer.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-990">상태 시스템과 순서도 워크플로에서 활동 및 전환의 자동 연결 및 자동 삽입</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-990">Auto-connect and auto-insert for activities and transitions in state machine and flowchart workflows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-991">XAML 파일의 단일 요소에 워크플로의 뷰 상태 정보가 저장되므로 뷰 상태 정보를 쉽게 찾아 편집할 수 있음</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-991">Storage of the view state information for a workflow in a single element in the XAML file, so you can easily locate and edit the view state information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-992">자식 활동이 지속되지 않도록 하는 NoPersistScope 컨테이너 활동</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-992">A NoPersistScope container activity to prevent child activities from persisting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-993">C# 식에 대한 지원</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-993">Support for C# expressions:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-994">Visual Basic을 사용하는 워크플로 프로젝트에서는 Visual Basic 식을 사용하고, C# 워크플로 프로젝트에서는 C# 식을 사용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-994">Workflow projects that use Visual Basic will use Visual Basic expressions, and C# workflow projects will use C# expressions.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-995">Visual Studio 2010에서 만들어지고 Visual Basic 식이 있는 C# 워크플로 프로젝트는 C# 식을 사용하는 C# 워크플로 프로젝트와 호환됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-995">C# workflow projects that were created in Visual Studio 2010 and that have Visual Basic expressions are compatible with C# workflow projects that use C# expressions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-996">버전 관리 향상</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-996">Versioning enhancements:</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-997">지속되는 워크플로 인스턴스와 해당 워크플로 정의 사이에 매핑을 제공하는 새로운 <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> 클래스</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-997">The new  <xref:System.Activities.WorkflowIdentity> class, which provides a mapping between a persisted workflow instance and its workflow definition.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-998"><xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>를 포함하여 같은 호스트에서 여러 워크플로 버전을 side-by-side로 실행</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-998">Side-by-side execution of multiple workflow versions in the same host, including <xref:System.ServiceModel.Activities.WorkflowServiceHost>.</span></span>

    - <span data-ttu-id="63064-999">동적 업데이트에서 지속된 워크플로 인스턴스의 정의를 수정할 수 있는 기능</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-999">In Dynamic Update, the ability to modify the definition of a persisted workflow instance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="63064-1000">기존 서비스 계약과 일치하도록 자동 생성 활동에 대한 지원을 제공하는 계약 중심 워크플로 서비스 개발</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1000">Contract-first workflow service development, which provides support for automatically generating activities to match an existing service contract.</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="63064-1001">자세한 내용은 [Windows Workflow Foundation의 새로운 기능](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176)을 참조하십시오.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1001">For more information, see [What's New in Windows Workflow Foundation](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228176).</span></span>

<a name="tailored"></a> 
### [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]
 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)]<span data-ttu-id="63064-1002"> 응용 프로그램은 특정 폼 팩터용으로 설계되었으며 Windows 운영 체제의 강력한 기능을 활용합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1002"> apps are designed for specific form factors and leverage the power of the Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-1003">[!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] 또는 4.5.1의 하위 집합은 C# 또는 Visual Basic을 사용하여 Windows용 [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] 응용 프로그램을 빌드하는 데 사용할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1003">A subset of the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] or 4.5.1 is available for building [!INCLUDE[win8_appname_long](../../../includes/win8-appname-long-md.md)] apps for Windows by using C# or Visual Basic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-1004">이 하위 집합을 [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]이라고 하며 Windows 개발자 센터의 [개요](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491)에 설명되어 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1004">This subset is called [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)] and is discussed in an [overview](http://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=228491) in the Windows Dev Center.</span></span>

<a name="portable"></a> 
### <a name="portable-class-libraries"></a><span data-ttu-id="63064-1005">이식 가능한 클래스 라이브러리</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1005">Portable Class Libraries</span></span>
 <span data-ttu-id="63064-1006">[!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] 및 이후 버전의 이식 가능한 클래스 라이브러리 프로젝트를 사용하여 여러 .NET Framework 플랫폼에서 작동하는 관리되는 어셈블리를 작성하고 빌드할 수 있습니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1006">The Portable Class Library project in [!INCLUDE[vs_dev11_long](../../../includes/vs-dev11-long-md.md)] (and later versions) enables you to write and build managed assemblies that work on multiple .NET Framework platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-1007">이식 가능한 클래스 라이브러리 프로젝트를 사용하여 대상 플랫폼(예: Windows Phone 및 [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)])을 선택합니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1007">Using a Portable Class Library project, you choose the platforms (such as Windows Phone and [!INCLUDE[net_win8_profile](../../../includes/net-win8-profile-md.md)]) to target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-1008">프로젝트에서 사용할 수 있는 형식 및 멤버는 이러한 플랫폼에서 공용 형식 및 멤버로 자동으로 제한됩니다.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1008">The available types and members in your project are automatically restricted to the common types and members across these platforms.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="63064-1009">자세한 내용은 [이식 가능한 클래스 라이브러리](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md)를 참조하십시오.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="63064-1009">For more information, see [Portable Class Library](../../../docs/standard/cross-platform/cross-platform-development-with-the-portable-class-library.md).</span></span>
